<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Slavonic Dances
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Slovanské tance
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Dvo%C5%99%C3%A1k,_Anton%C3%ADn" title="Category:Dvořák, Antonín">Dvořák, Antonín</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.72&#160;; B.145 (Piano duet), B.147 (Orchestration)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IAD 82
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>8 dances:<br /><i>These are sometimes numbered from 9 to 16, as a continuation of the <a href="/wiki/Slavonic_Dances,_Op.46_(Dvo%C5%99%C3%A1k,_Anton%C3%ADn)" title="Slavonic Dances, Op.46 (Dvořák, Antonín)">Op.46</a> series.</i>
<ol><li> (9). <i>Odzemek</i>. Vivace (B major)
</li><li> (10). <i>Dumka</i>. Allegretto grazioso (E minor)
</li><li> (11). <i>Skocná</i>. Allegro (F major)
</li><li> (12). <i>Dumka</i>. Allegretto grazioso (D<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span> major)
</li><li> (13). <i>Spacírka</i>. Poco Adagio—Vivace (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span> minor)
</li><li> (14). <i>Polonaise</i>. Moderato, quasi menuetto (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span> major)
</li><li> (15). <i>Kolo</i>. Allegro vivace (C major)
</li><li> (16). <i>Sousedská</i>. Grazioso e lento, ma non troppo, quasi tempo di Valse (A<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span> major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1886 (June-July) - <i>Piano duet</i><br />1886-87 – <i>Orchestration</i>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1887-01-06 in Prague (Nos.9, 10, 15) – <i>Orchestration</i>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1886 (Piano duet), 1887 (Orchestration)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>piano 4 hands or orchestra <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<dl><dd>piccolo, 2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 clarinets, 2 bassoons<br />4 horns, 2 trumpets, 3 trombones<br />timpani, bass drum, cymbals, triangle, glockenspiel, strings </div>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
